 Shoes need special care in winter
 juuton ko surakshit rakhane vaala spray yaa vaix aapke juuton kii umr badha saktaa he
 By adopting some such easy measures, you can keep the shoes safe in winter
 
 
 - sardiyon aane par juuton ko surakshit rakhana aapaki praathamikta hoti he
 You can protect the shoes by spraying them
 - ghar aate hi juuton ko nami se bachaane ke liye ghode ke baalo se bane brush yaa akhbaar ke kaagaj se saaf karen
 Be sure to polish with shoe wax on leather shoes
 yah juuton kii chamak barkaraar rakhata he agar aap ek hafte se zyada samay se juute nahin pahan rahe hai to phir ise mote kaagaj yaa box se dhak kar rakhen
 - Use vinegar (vinegar) to get rid of stains on shoes and rub them with cotton swabs
 tippaniyan - Clean your feet before wearing shoes, because there is a possibility of mold inside them due to moisture or bad shoes
 - halki nami hone par juuton ko radiator yaa heater se nahin sukhaana chahie kyonki isse juute fat sakate hai
 - Keeping the shoes safe is your priority when winter comes
 aap juuton ke upar spray lagaakar use surakshit rakh sakate hai
 To protect the shoes from moisture, come clean with a brush or newspaper made of horse hair
 - chamade ke juuton par shu vaix se polish karnaa nahin bhoolen
 It keeps the shine of the shoes
 If you have not been wearing shoes for more than a week, then cover it with thick paper or box
 - juuton par pade daag-dhabbe chhudaane ke liye vinegar (sirka) kaa istemaal kar rooyee ke phahe se ragadkar chhudaayein
